Environment: The hotel location is not as good as Phoenix International Hotel, and it is not very convenient to eat.

But the breakfast is very poor, with very few varieties, no noodle stalls, fried rice is spicy, purple sweet potatoes are particularly unpalatable, and there is no self-service freshly ground coffee. The only advantage is that the floor is high and the view is good.
In short, the facilities and services are five-star, and the breakfast is three-star
